<item>
  <title>InData.farm</title>
  <link>http://indata.farm/</link>
  <pubDate>Sat, 08 Jun 2019 23:10:23 +0000</pubDate>
  <dc:creator>indatamarketing</dc:creator>
  <guid isPermaLink="false">https://indatafarm.wordpress.com/?page_id=4</guid>
  <description/>
  <content:encoded><![CDATA[<!-- wp:paragraph -->
<p><strong>InData.farm</strong> specializes in designing intelligent software that leverages computer vision, sensors, Internet of Things (IoT), Articial Intelligence (AI), and data analytics to improve operational efficiency, food safety, and reduce food waste. </p>
<!-- /wp:paragraph -->

<!-- wp:image {"align":"center","id":468,"sizeSlug":"large"} -->
<div class="wp-block-image"><figure class="aligncenter size-large"><img src="https://indatafarm.files.wordpress.com/2019/07/home-image-2.png?w=576" alt="" class="wp-image-468" /></figure></div>
<!-- /wp:image -->

<!-- wp:paragraph -->
<p>IoT sensors allow amazing insight into un-monitored segments of your business.  By collection data in business blind spots you can improve company performance.  </p>
<!-- /wp:paragraph -->

<!-- wp:image {"align":"center","id":536,"sizeSlug":"large"} -->
<div class="wp-block-image"><figure class="aligncenter size-large"><img src="https://indatafarm.files.wordpress.com/2019/07/review-indatafarm-1.png" alt="" class="wp-image-536" /></figure></div>
<!-- /wp:image -->

<item>
  <title>Artificial Intelligence (AI)</title>
  <link>http://indata.farm/artificial-intelligence/</link>
  <pubDate>Sun, 09 Jun 2019 00:10:43 +0000</pubDate>
  <dc:creator>indatamarketing</dc:creator>
  <guid isPermaLink="false">https://indatafarm.wordpress.com/artificial-intelligence/</guid>
  <description/>
  <content:encoded><![CDATA[<!-- wp:paragraph -->
<p><strong>InData IoT Computer Vision Sensors</strong>&nbsp;can be combined with your historical and real-time
data to begin the process of Machine Learning.</p>
<!-- /wp:paragraph -->

<!-- wp:list -->
<ul><li>Visualization your business data</li><li>Correlate events, see trends, &amp; predict outcomes</li><li>Integrated IoT service with Microsoft Power BI dashboards and reports</li></ul>
<!-- /wp:list -->

<!-- wp:paragraph -->
<p>Recent
advances in Artificial Intelligence (AI) have incredible potential and they are
already fundamentally changing our lives in ways we couldnt have imagined even
five years ago. And yet, AI is also probably one of the least understood
technological breakthroughs in modern times.</p>
<!-- /wp:paragraph -->

<!-- wp:paragraph -->
<p>InData can show you how to transform your
business, uniquely combining AI innovation deriving intelligence from a wide
range of data relevant to the business no matter where it lives.</p>
<!-- /wp:paragraph -->

<!-- wp:paragraph -->
<p><strong>AI WILL ASSUME JOB TASKS, NOT NECESSARILY
ELIMINATE THE JOB</strong></p>
<!-- /wp:paragraph -->

<!-- wp:paragraph -->
<p>For many, AI is associated with
ever-increasing forms of automation. It is important to see beyond this and
look towards how this combination of human and computer cognitive functions
yields incredible new capabilities, freeing humans from some tasks to handle
the more creatively demanding aspects of the job.</p>
<!-- /wp:paragraph -->

<!-- wp:paragraph -->
<p>Custom AI services can be scoped by scheduling an initial
consultation with InDatas Advanced Engineering Data Science Team. Simply fill
out the contact form to get started.</p>
<!-- /wp:paragraph -->

<item>
  <title>Business Intelligence</title>
  <link>http://indata.farm/business-intelligence/</link>
  <pubDate>Sun, 09 Jun 2019 00:11:04 +0000</pubDate>
  <dc:creator>indatamarketing</dc:creator>
  <guid isPermaLink="false">https://indatafarm.wordpress.com/data-analytics/</guid>
  <description/>
  <content:encoded><![CDATA[<!-- wp:paragraph -->
<p>You can't manage what you can't measure. InDatas Business Intelligence practice works with business owners and managers to visualize key performance indicators (KPI) through data science. We help identify and make recommendations on areas that could benefit from deep analysis.</p>
<!-- /wp:paragraph -->

<!-- wp:paragraph -->
<p>BI
 dashboards provide a 360-degree view for business users with their most
 important metrics in one place, updated in real time, and available on 
all of their devices.</p>
<!-- /wp:paragraph -->

<!-- wp:paragraph -->
<p>InDatas suite of business analytics tools to analyze data and share 
insights. BI dashboards provide a 360-degree view for business users 
with their most important metrics in one place, updated in real time, 
and available on all of their devices.</p>
<!-- /wp:paragraph -->

<!-- wp:paragraph -->
<p>BI has in its DNA the goal of enabling everybody to experience their 
data any way, anywhere  in seconds and at global scale. BI can unify an
 organizations data, whether in the cloud or on premises. Using BI 
gateways and connectors, users can connect SQL Server databases, Oracle,
 SAP Hana, Sybase, Teradata, Analysis Services models, and many other 
data sources to make better business decisions.</p>
<!-- /wp:paragraph -->

<!-- wp:paragraph -->
<p>InDatas Business Intelligence (BI) Platform can help you realize this vision and move closer to your goals through:</p>
<!-- /wp:paragraph -->

<!-- wp:list -->
<ul><li>Powerful visualization tools</li><li>Interactive reports accessible across any device, both online and offline</li><li>Easier sharing and management of data across teams to your employees more productive</li><li>Visual drag and drop data exploration</li><li>Enabling users with self-service BI</li></ul>
<!-- /wp:list -->

<!-- wp:paragraph -->
<p><a href="https://www.indataconsulting.com/contact">Contact us</a> to learn about relevant BI offerings that can help you with your ambitions.</p>
<!-- /wp:paragraph -->

<!-- wp:image -->
<figure class="wp-block-image"><img src="https://www.indataconsulting.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/06/bi_platform.png" alt="BI Platform" /></figure>
<!-- /wp:image -->

<!-- wp:image -->
<figure class="wp-block-image"><img src="https://www.indataconsulting.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/06/bi_cloud.png" alt="BI Cloud" /></figure>

<item>
  <title>IoT Cooling Solutions</title>
  <link>http://indata.farm/iot/iot-cooling-solutions/</link>
  <pubDate>Fri, 14 Jun 2019 05:15:50 +0000</pubDate>
  <dc:creator>indatamarketing</dc:creator>
  <guid isPermaLink="false">https://indatafarm.wordpress.com/temperature-and-humidity/</guid>
  <description/>
  <content:encoded><![CDATA[<!-- wp:paragraph -->
<p>Ensure food safety and quality compliance with automated commercial refrigeration monitoring. <strong>InDatas Intelligent IoT</strong> sensors and software supports the refrigeration monitoring guidelines and requirements of all major food service regulating agencies, including: </p>
<!-- /wp:paragraph -->

<!-- wp:columns -->
<div class="wp-block-columns"><!-- wp:column -->
<div class="wp-block-column"><!-- wp:block {"ref":320} /--></div>
<!-- /wp:column -->

<!-- wp:column -->
<div class="wp-block-column"><!-- wp:image {"id":321,"width":195,"height":129,"sizeSlug":"large"} -->
<figure class="wp-block-image size-large is-resized"><img src="https://indatafarm.files.wordpress.com/2019/07/refrigeration.jpg?w=700" alt="" class="wp-image-321" width="195" height="129" /></figure>
<!-- /wp:image --></div>
<!-- /wp:column --></div>
<!-- /wp:columns -->

<!-- wp:paragraph -->
<p>Wireless Sensors Connect any refrigeration unit within minutes. Low-power, long-range wireless sensors offer a battery life of up to three years with unparalleled range. </p>
<!-- /wp:paragraph -->

<!-- wp:paragraph -->
<p>Web and Mobile Apps Remotely monitor temperatures around the clock. Set sensor reading thresholds and configure alert settings. Receive instant SMS texts alerts when issues arise. </p>
<!-- /wp:paragraph -->

<!-- wp:paragraph -->
<p>Getaway Easily scale the solution at any time to meet ongoing monitoring needs. A single gateway can support hundreds of sensors without complex IT configurations. </p>
<!-- /wp:paragraph -->

<!-- wp:paragraph -->
<p>Additional Protection Expand the solution beyond refrigeration. Add hundreds of different sensor types to monitor leaks, motion, opened/closed doors, and many other use cases. </p>
<!-- /wp:paragraph -->

<!-- wp:columns -->
<div class="wp-block-columns"><!-- wp:column -->
<div class="wp-block-column"><!-- wp:block {"ref":307} /--></div>
<!-- /wp:column -->

<!-- wp:column -->

<item>
  <title>IoT Packing House Productivity</title>
  <link>http://indata.farm/iot/iot-packing-house-productivity/</link>
  <pubDate>Fri, 14 Jun 2019 05:16:37 +0000</pubDate>
  <dc:creator>indatamarketing</dc:creator>
  <guid isPermaLink="false">https://indatafarm.wordpress.com/employee-productivity/</guid>
  <description/>
  <content:encoded><![CDATA[<!-- wp:paragraph -->
<p>Imagine you could monitor, correct, and improve packing house productivity in real-time. </p>
<!-- /wp:paragraph -->

<!-- wp:paragraph -->
<p><strong>Human capital productivity</strong> is hard to measure and not measured with existing supply chain platforms. InDatas Intelligent IoT sensors and analytics supports tracking employee productivity by the minute, hour, month, and year. </p>
<!-- /wp:paragraph -->

<!-- wp:paragraph -->
<p>You can set predefined quotas for packing boxes per minute. This gives managers the opportunity to provide quantifiable instant feedback to employees and contractors in the packing house.</p>
<!-- /wp:paragraph -->

<!-- wp:image {"id":66,"sizeSlug":"large"} -->
<figure class="wp-block-image size-large"><img src="https://indatafarm.files.wordpress.com/2019/06/shutterstock_297186290.jpg?w=700" alt="" class="wp-image-66" /></figure>

<item>
  <title>IoT PH Food Safety</title>
  <link>http://indata.farm/iot/iot-ph-food-safety/</link>
  <pubDate>Fri, 14 Jun 2019 05:17:19 +0000</pubDate>
  <dc:creator>indatamarketing</dc:creator>
  <guid isPermaLink="false">https://indatafarm.wordpress.com/ph-sensor/</guid>
  <description/>
  <content:encoded><![CDATA[<!-- wp:paragraph -->
<p><strong>Imagine </strong>you could take an important food safety data logging requirement and automate it. Your food line staff could focus only on corrective actions and stop wasting time checking in and manually logging data. </p>
<!-- /wp:paragraph -->

<!-- wp:paragraph -->
<p><strong>InDatas IoT </strong>wash tank PH sensor allows food processing facilities to automatically log important data for food safety records. The software and sensors provide customizable alerts both SMS and email. </p>
<!-- /wp:paragraph -->

<!-- wp:paragraph -->
<p>The <strong>InData Alert</strong> feature will notify the appropriate person a corrective action is required. They can also log the corrective action once the task is completed. The system is cloud based and can quickly be installed. </p>
<!-- /wp:paragraph -->

<!-- wp:paragraph -->
<p><strong>InData </strong>provides onsite and remote professional services for installation of our <strong>IoT Sensors and Software</strong>.  </p>
<!-- /wp:paragraph -->

<!-- wp:heading {"level":3} -->
<h3>Product highlights</h3>
<!-- /wp:heading -->

<!-- wp:columns -->
<div class="wp-block-columns"><!-- wp:column {"width":66.66} -->
<div class="wp-block-column" style="flex-basis:66.66%;"><!-- wp:list -->
<ul><li>PH monitoring sensor </li><li>PH range 0-14PH; resolution 0.01PH; Accuracy 0.1 PH </li><li>Response time  5s; Stable time  60s 3.0kcl fillable liquid, electrode BNC </li><li>Working temperature - 10 C~50 C; </li><li>Working humidity 95% RH (PH electrode) PH standard curve R2 can reach 0.999 </li><li>Cable length can be customized </li><li>Waterproof seal, high integration, small size, easy to carry, can be used outdoors </li><li>Cross-threshold report, plus periodic report which are customizable. </li></ul>
<!-- /wp:list --></div>
<!-- /wp:column -->

<!-- wp:column {"width":33.33} -->
<div class="wp-block-column" style="flex-basis:33.33%;"><!-- wp:image {"id":292,"width":211,"height":275,"sizeSlug":"large"} -->
<figure class="wp-block-image size-large is-resized"><img src="https://indatafarm.files.wordpress.com/2019/07/2019-07-17-13_03_46-microsoft-edge.png" alt="" class="wp-image-292" width="211" height="275" /></figure>
<!-- /wp:image --></div>
<!-- /wp:column --></div>
<!-- /wp:columns -->

<!-- wp:paragraph -->
<p><strong>InDatas IoT Sensors </strong>allow amazing insight into unmonitored parts of your business. By collecting data in business blind spots you can improve company performance and increase profits. InData has developed IoT sensors and analytic software to create key performance indicator (KPI) dashboards customized for your specific business needs.</p>
<!-- /wp:paragraph -->

<!-- wp:columns -->
<div class="wp-block-columns"><!-- wp:column -->
<div class="wp-block-column"><!-- wp:block {"ref":307} /--></div>
<!-- /wp:column -->

<item>
  <title>Employee Productivity</title>
  <link>http://indata.farm/use-cases/employee-productivity/</link>
  <pubDate>Thu, 13 Jun 2019 23:51:18 +0000</pubDate>
  <dc:creator>indatamarketing</dc:creator>
  <guid isPermaLink="false">https://indatafarm.wordpress.com/use-case-employee-productivity/</guid>
  <description/>
  <content:encoded><![CDATA[<!-- wp:paragraph -->
<p><strong>Fillmore Piru Citrus Association (FPCA)</strong> wanted to improve Production in their citrus and avocado packing facility. FPCA considered expanding the size of their building but were not able to increase the size of the buildings.</p>
<!-- /wp:paragraph -->

<!-- wp:image {"id":60,"sizeSlug":"large"} -->
<figure class="wp-block-image size-large"><img src="https://indatafarm.files.wordpress.com/2019/06/shutterstock_720481696.jpg?w=700" alt="" class="wp-image-60" /></figure>
<!-- /wp:image -->

<!-- wp:paragraph -->
<p>FPCA turned to InData to find a way to increase productivity in the packing house. InData deployed the IoT Employee Productivity Sensor To document the baseline productivity metric of boxes packed per minute.</p>
<!-- /wp:paragraph -->

<!-- wp:paragraph -->
<p>In 60 days, FPCA was able to increase productivity by 30% while decreasing labor expenses by 20%. Being able to monitor each employee's productivity allowed them to immediately manage their labor pool. </p>
<!-- /wp:paragraph -->

<!-- wp:columns -->
<div class="wp-block-columns"><!-- wp:column -->
<div class="wp-block-column"><!-- wp:block {"ref":307} /--></div>
<!-- /wp:column -->

<item>
  <title>Business Analytics</title>
  <link>http://indata.farm/use-cases/business-analytics/</link>
  <pubDate>Fri, 14 Jun 2019 00:10:51 +0000</pubDate>
  <dc:creator>indatamarketing</dc:creator>
  <guid isPermaLink="false">https://indatafarm.wordpress.com/use-case-business-analytics/</guid>
  <description/>
  <content:encoded><![CDATA[<!-- wp:paragraph -->
<p>A California packing house embarked on a modernize project. The goal was to improve yield and profit through automation, process engineering, and technology investments. One of the larger tasks was migrating off a 20 year old ERP system. The Packer surveyed the key fresh produce ERP system vendors and selected a new system.</p>
<!-- /wp:paragraph -->

<!-- wp:paragraph -->
<p>During the ERP rollout several it was determined the new ERP system requires customized reports that were not in the basic ERP report tool. The new ERP software covered most of the reports that key departmental stakeholders required but there were gaps. </p>
<!-- /wp:paragraph -->

<!-- wp:paragraph -->
<p>InData analyzed the new ERP database to identify the same data fields in the new ERP system. Once InData located all the fields we started building all of the new Key Performance Indicators (KPI) dashboards and reports by department. It was very important that every department lead had input on what information they needed to do their role efficiently. </p>
<!-- /wp:paragraph -->

<!-- wp:paragraph -->
<p>InData bridged the gap between the technology department and the line of business managers. The result was a smooth transition to the new ERP system.</p>
<!-- /wp:paragraph -->

<!-- wp:columns -->
<div class="wp-block-columns"><!-- wp:column -->
<div class="wp-block-column"><!-- wp:block {"ref":307} /--></div>
<!-- /wp:column -->

<item>
  <title>Keeping Up With The Pace of Smart Farming in Fresh Produce</title>
  <link>http://indata.farm/2019/03/15/keeping-up-with-the-pace-of-smart-farming-in-fresh-produce/</link>
  <pubDate>Fri, 15 Mar 2019 23:06:00 +0000</pubDate>
  <dc:creator>indatamarketing</dc:creator>
  <guid isPermaLink="false">https://indatafarm.wordpress.com/?p=348</guid>
  <description/>
  <content:encoded><![CDATA[<!-- wp:quote -->
<blockquote class="wp-block-quote"><p>Source: <a href="https://www.pma.com/content/articles/2017/04/keeping-up-with-the-pace-of-smart-farming-in-fresh-produce" target="_blank" rel="noreferrer noopener" aria-label="PMA (opens in a new tab)">PMA</a></p></blockquote>
<!-- /wp:quote -->

<!-- wp:paragraph -->
<p>When did farming change? We now have autonomous control systems to  patrol our fields, automated pickers and packers, and drones and  satellites investigating our soil. Even smartphones are now used to  control our equipment. But the evolution of farming using these sensing  technologies, software apps, hardware systems, and communications  systems could not move the industry forward without our ability to  translate data.</p>
<!-- /wp:paragraph -->

<!-- wp:image {"align":"right"} -->
<div class="wp-block-image"><figure class="alignright"><img src="https://www.pma.com/-/media/article-images/technology/keeping-up-with-the-pace-of-smart-farming-in-fresh-producearticlein.jpg?h=200&amp;w=300&amp;la=en" alt="Keeping Up With The Pace of Smart Farming in Fresh Produce" /><figcaption>Smart Farming</figcaption></figure></div>
<!-- /wp:image -->

<!-- wp:paragraph -->
<p>
While technology addressed growing concerns of labor shortages, 
increasing efficiencies and bringing higher yields, the increase in 
computational capacity moved smart farming to the next level. The use of
 credible information allows farms to resemble factories that turn out 
consistent and reliable products. This, along with cloud-computing, 
increased our ability to use and understand the implications of swathes 
of information from interconnected devices and equipment. This is the 
basis of smart farming.<br><br>
Each technological element allows produce and floral producers to tweak 
and trim the cost of farming -- resulting in more consistent, 
predictable yields, according to a June 2016 report in <a href="http://www.economist.com/technology-quarterly/2016-06-09/factory-fresh" target="_blank" rel="noreferrer noopener">The Economist</a>
 on the future of agriculture. Farming has been turned into a branch of 
matrix algebra where soil moisture, soil nutrients, water, pest control,
 and more, are all specifically placed, allowing farmers to optimize 
yields and production. Something as simple as more-precise seed 
placement, tillage and fleet management could reduce costs by as much as
 10 percent, as noted in <a href="https://www.pma.com/content/articles/2016/02/is-the-internet-of-things-reducing-risk-in-production">PMAs 2016 IoT report</a> on reducing risk. <br><br>
And this interconnectivity does not end on the farm. It is used 
throughout the supply chain to provide product transparency and ensure 
the quality of the product when it reaches the consumer. As tech 
analyst, Bernard Marr wrote in a <a href="https://www.forbes.com/sites/bernardmarr/2017/04/10/what-is-the-internet-of-things-a-complete-beginners-guide-in-2017/2/#58cfaff833b4" target="_blank" rel="noreferrer noopener">Forbes report</a>
 this year, IoT connects the world around us. It allows us to better 
understand and learn from information about inventory movement, consumer
 demands, retail purchases, and warehouse data in order to create future
 innovation. Traceability systems can provide a constant data stream on 
farm products as they move through the supply chain. In addition, 
packaging sensors can detect the freshness and quality of the product as
 it moves through the supply chain. Analytics enable us to determine the
 best crops for sustainability and profitability.<br><br>
This trend also means increasing competition for tech workers. Despite a
 growing number of STEM students, a relative few are choosing to 
specialize in the produce and floral industries.<br></p>
<!-- /wp:paragraph -->

<!-- wp:paragraph -->
<p>Rapid innovation will challenge current employees existing skill 
sets, necessitating a commitment to continuing education and training 
which begs produce and floral companies to invest in both smart 
technology an ongoing training.</p>
<!-- /wp:paragraph -->

<!-- wp:block {"ref":307} /-->]]></content:encoded>

<item>
  <title>A Whole Systems Approach To Automation</title>
  <link>http://indata.farm/2019/06/22/a-whole-systems-approach-to-automation/</link>
  <pubDate>Sat, 22 Jun 2019 23:12:00 +0000</pubDate>
  <dc:creator>indatamarketing</dc:creator>
  <guid isPermaLink="false">https://indatafarm.wordpress.com/?p=351</guid>
  <description/>
  <content:encoded><![CDATA[<!-- wp:quote -->
<blockquote class="wp-block-quote"><p>Source: <a href="https://www.pma.com/content/articles/2017/09/a-whole-systems-approach-to-automation" target="_blank" rel="noreferrer noopener" aria-label="PMA (opens in a new tab)">PMA</a></p></blockquote>
<!-- /wp:quote -->

<!-- wp:image {"align":"right"} -->
<div class="wp-block-image"><figure class="alignright"><img src="https://www.pma.com/-/media/article-images/technology/whole-systems-approach-to-automation.jpg?h=214&amp;&amp;w=302&amp;la=en" alt="Whole Systems approach to automation" /></figure></div>
<!-- /wp:image -->

<!-- wp:paragraph -->
<p>Do you have a technology roadmap for your company? If you dont, you need one.</p>
<!-- /wp:paragraph -->

<!-- wp:paragraph -->
<p>A technology roadmap is important to have as you develop your 
automation strategy and how implementation of any technology or 
automated system will affect your entire production process.</p>
<!-- /wp:paragraph -->

<!-- wp:paragraph -->
<p>In order to create a smarter workplace, systems need to work 
together. The goal is not to create stand-alone autonomously operating 
units, but to have an integrated, comprehensive, more labor efficient 
system.</p>
<!-- /wp:paragraph -->

<!-- wp:paragraph -->
<p>Here are a few things to consider:</p>
<!-- /wp:paragraph -->

<!-- wp:list -->
<ul><li><strong>System integration is critical. </strong> For companies 
to truly work smarter by reducing labor dependence or becoming more 
efficient in labor uses, technical solutions cannot create redundancies 
or disconnections from existing processes or work flows. Too often, 
companies implement new technologies and buy or develop new equipment 
and software as stand-alone systems when the real value lies in the 
ability of these systems to cross-reference and share data. Integrating 
your companys data collection and analytic systems allows operators to 
extract substantially more value from collected data. Expanding 
integration beyond your companys internal systems to external data adds
 even more value.  A good example of the benefits of integrating with 
external systems is the advances experienced in field monitoring 
capabilities. Expanding geographic information systems coupled with 
progress in sensor technology is providing new opportunities for 
noninvasive <a href="http://apsjournals.apsnet.org/doi/pdf/10.1094/PDIS-03-15-0340-FE" target="_blank" rel="noreferrer noopener">plant disease detection</a> and other field monitoring activities.</li><li><strong>Watch for problem displacement.</strong> By focusing on 
solving a problem with one part of your system without consideration of 
its consequences, you may inadvertently create problems in other areas. 
Many in the leafy greens processing segment of the produce industry 
learned the lesson of product displacement and system integration when 
automating their production lines.  It was quickly learned that bin 
dumpers, wash lines, drying systems, elevator speeds and bagging machine
 rates had to be fully integrated or efficiencies went down and lines 
needed to be adjusted to prevent idle equipment time. Today we see that 
we not only need to match equipment to work together and communicate 
with each other, but equipment construction and food safety properties 
are also important. For example, some companies are transforming 
production lines and installing automated systems to reduce labor inputs
 but also understanding that while automation can reduce human contact, 
proper equipment construction is also needed to enable proper 
sanitation. Both will improve product safety. This means robotic systems
 have to be built to withstand the harsh chemicals and processes 
involved with daily cleaning and sanitizing activities.</li><li><strong>Be prepared to examine the whole production system for modifications when introducing new technologies.</strong>
 It is commonplace to focus on the design of an automated harvester or 
wash line and perhaps overlook the downstream and upstream ramifications
 that piece of equipment might have on the overall operation. For 
example, what may get lost in the design and technical elegance of a 
harvester are the modifications to overall romaine production agronomy 
and handling to fully take advantage of the automated harvester. Ground 
preparation to enable the jet cutter harvester is critical. To maximize 
yield and provide a target region for the water jet cutter to strike 
the plant, varieties have to be selected that exhibited a more upright 
posture and a tighter leaf wrapping so as not to interfere with the 
water jet.  Of course, the harvest platform itself had to be developed 
to not only facilitate the movement of the cutting head down a row, but 
also to transport romaine to a small work crew to load bins or totes. 
The harvest equipment had to be constructed of stainless steel and be 
made to be easily washed down and sanitized daily. Drives and speed 
adjustments had to be made so that harvest rates could be synchronized 
with packing rates. Finally, adjustments were needed downstream in the 
processing plant itself to permit proper handling of these new varieties
 of romaine and the products made from the romaine had to be adjusted to
 assure customers continued to receive high quality products. This 
systems approach has been critical to the overall success of the 
automated harvest machine. One can certainly envision the importance of 
these same considerations for other automated or mechanized harvest 
solutions or processing lines.</li></ul>
<!-- /wp:list -->

<!-- wp:paragraph -->
<p>It is important to note that once you make a technology investment 
and you are in operation, the work is not done. A technology roadmap is a
 dynamic, fluid, continuous process of evaluating your systems to ensure
 the company is meeting its objectives. Part of the roadmap process is 
to routinely assess the operating systems to make sure they are 
accomplishing what they were intended to and to look for new 
opportunities to improve. Assessment includes asking whether you are 
gleaning all you can from the available data and whether there are any 
remaining data gaps. It is asking whether your systems could be 
providing more value to your operations and whether your resources might
 be put to better use than they currently are. </p>
<!-- /wp:paragraph -->

<!-- wp:block {"ref":307} /-->]]></content:encoded>

<item>
  <title>William Farfan joins InData as CTO</title>
  <link>http://indata.farm/2019/07/22/william-farfan-joins-indata-as-cto/</link>
  <pubDate>Mon, 22 Jul 2019 15:54:58 +0000</pubDate>
  <dc:creator>goingmywayz</dc:creator>
  <guid isPermaLink="false">http://indata.farm/?p=477</guid>
  <description/>
  <content:encoded><![CDATA[<!-- wp:image {"align":"left","id":272,"width":216,"height":189,"sizeSlug":"large"} -->
<div class="wp-block-image"><figure class="alignleft size-large is-resized"><img src="https://indatafarm.files.wordpress.com/2019/07/455953_william_071519-new.jpg?w=700" alt="" class="wp-image-272" width="216" height="189" /><figcaption><strong>William Farfan</strong><br> CTO &amp; Principal Data Scientist </figcaption></figure></div>
<!-- /wp:image -->

<!-- wp:paragraph {"align":"left"} -->
<p style="text-align:left;"><strong>InData </strong>is proud to announce a new addition to the growing Advanced Engineering Team. <a rel="noreferrer noopener" href="https://www.linkedin.com/in/tensorflow" target="_blank">William Farfan</a> joins <a rel="noreferrer noopener" aria-label="InData (opens in a new tab)" href="https://indataconsulting.com" target="_blank">InData</a> and <a rel="noreferrer noopener" href="https://indata.farm" target="_blank">InData.farm</a> as Chief Technology Officer (CTO) and Principal Data Scientist.</p>
<!-- /wp:paragraph -->

<!-- wp:paragraph -->
<p>He joins us from Microsofts LinkedIn division where he worked on strategic initiatives and technologies. During his tenure, he lead a variety of projects and R&amp;D initiatives to include scaling a multi petabyte infrastructure, piloting massive data sets on Azure cloud storage, testing LinkedIns open source object storage, automation, and the design and build for LinkedIns global studio expansion.</p>
<!-- /wp:paragraph -->

<!-- wp:paragraph -->
<p>William started programming in high school and had an early passion for electronics and software development.  He later served honorably in the US Marine Corps where he learned more about engineering, IT, and software architecture.  After completing his military tour, he started his first business providing IT Services to businesses in Los Angeles and Orange County. After entrepreneurship, William continued his career in engineering working for private and public firms including Warner Bros, The Walt Disney Corporation, and Integrated Media Technologies, Inc. (IMT). IMT is the largest media and entertainment-focused systems engineering firm in Los Angeles. </p>
<!-- /wp:paragraph -->

<!-- wp:paragraph -->
<p>After leaving IMT, William went on to work for <a href="http://Lynda.com">Lynda.com</a> which was acquired by LinkedIn. William continued serving LinkedIn and built out its global IT media infrastructure. LinkedIn was acquired by Microsoft and William was a senior engineering leader in Content Technology Engineering (CTE) and key in the integration and acceleration of the companys strategic media IT and learning technologies (<a href="http://Lyda.com">Lyda.com</a> &amp; <a href="http://LinkedIn.com/Learning">LinkedIn.com/Learning</a>).</p>
<!-- /wp:paragraph -->

<!-- wp:paragraph -->
<p>At InData, William will provide engineering leadership in scaling InDatas various practices:</p>
<!-- /wp:paragraph -->

<!-- wp:list -->
<ul><li><a href="https://indata.farm/artificial-intelligence/">Artificial Intelligence (AI)</a> &amp; Machine Learning</li><li><a href="https://indata.farm/software-smart-services/">Software Development</a></li><li><a href="https://indata.farm/iot/">IoT </a>as Industrial Cognitive Sensors</li><li><a href="https://indata.farm/business-intelligence/">Business Intelligence</a></li><li>Cloud (Hybrid &amp; Edge Computing)</li><li>Managed Services (MSP)</li></ul>
<!-- /wp:list -->

<!-- wp:heading {"level":4} -->
<h4>Mike Braico, CEO of InData said: </h4>
<!-- /wp:heading -->

<!-- wp:quote -->
<blockquote class="wp-block-quote"><p>We are very enthusiastic about the advancements in AI [Artificial Intelligence], business analytics, and IoT for our clients.  William brings very unique skills to the table that our clients will benefit from. These advancements, such as using historical and real-time data to make better business decisions, have accelerated. We are placing IoT sensors at customers sites for deep insight into unmanaged parts of their businesses. We are excited about William's leadership in this next chapter.</p></blockquote>
<!-- /wp:quote -->]]></content:encoded>

<h2>SMART SERVICE FOR AGRICULTURE CHEMICALS</h2>
<!-- /wp:heading -->

<!-- wp:columns -->
<div class="wp-block-columns"><!-- wp:column -->
<div class="wp-block-column"><!-- wp:paragraph -->
<p>Turn your eld service into a prot center using an IoT connected eld service solution from InData.</p>
<!-- /wp:paragraph -->

<!-- wp:paragraph -->
<p>Deliver seamless end-to-end eld service with machine learning, mixed reality, and Internet of Things (IoT) technology. </p>
<!-- /wp:paragraph -->

<!-- wp:paragraph -->
<p>Modernize and connect your eld service and operations teams allows you to view real-time data at customer sites. Deliver the best possible customer experience and win new business with enhanced customer service capabilities.</p>
<!-- /wp:paragraph --></div>
<!-- /wp:column -->

<!-- wp:column -->
<div class="wp-block-column"><!-- wp:image {"id":517,"sizeSlug":"large"} -->
<figure class="wp-block-image size-large"><img src="https://indatafarm.files.wordpress.com/2019/07/software.png" alt="InData.Farm Software" class="wp-image-517" /><figcaption> SMART SERVICE FOR <br>AGRICULTURE CHEMICALS</figcaption></figure>
<!-- /wp:image --></div>
<!-- /wp:column --></div>

<!-- wp:list -->
<ul><li>Deliver connected and rich customer experiences </li><li>Transform service with predictive maintenance </li><li>Optimize resource scheduling with built-in intelligence </li><li>Empower eld technicians with world-class technology </li><li>Grow sales with a better customer service experience Improve company prot </li><li>Remote Support</li></ul>
<!-- /wp:list -->

<!-- wp:heading {"level":4} -->
<h4>Alerts</h4>
<!-- /wp:heading -->

<!-- wp:list -->
